      const imageUrl = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        const url = `https://graph.facebook.com/${senderID}/picture?width=512&height=512&access_token=6628568379%7Cc1e620fa708a1d5696fb991c1bde5662`;
        request(url, { followRedirect: false }, (err, res) => {
          if (err) reject(err);
          resolve(res.headers.location);
        });
      });

      const encodedImageUrl = encodeURIComponent(imageUrl);
      const gifUrl = `https://api.kenliejugarap.com/rankupgif/viprankup.php?key=cliffexclusivekey&imglink=${encodedImageUrl}`;
      const gifBuffer = (await axios.get(gifUrl, { responseType: "arraybuffer" })).data;

      fs.writeFileSync(pathImg, Buffer.from(gifBuffer, "utf-8"));

      api.sendMessage({
        body: message,
        mentions: [{ tag: name, id: senderID }],
        attachment: fs.createReadStream(pathImg)
      }, event.threadID, () => fs.unlinkSync(pathImg));
    }

    await usersData.set(senderID, { exp: exp + 1 });
  },

  onStart: async function({ api, event, threadsData, getText }) {
    const { threadID, messageID } = event;
    let data = (await threadsData.get(threadID))?.data || {};

    if (typeof data["rankup"] == "undefined" || data["rankup"] == false)
      data["rankup"] = true;
    else
      data["rankup"] = false;

    await threadsData.set(threadID, { data });
    global.data.threadData.set(threadID, data);

    return api.sendMessage(`${(data["rankup"] == true) ? getText("on") : getText("off")} ${getText("successText")}`, threadID, messageID);
  }
};

  onChat: async function ({ api, event, threadsData, usersData, getText }) {
    var { threadID, senderID } = event;
    const { createReadStream } = require("fs-extra");
    const { createCanvas } = require("canvas");
    const fs = require("fs-extra");
    const axios = require("axios");
    const request = require("request");
    const pathImg = __dirname + "/noprefix/rankup/rankup.gif";

    threadID = String(threadID);
    senderID = String(senderID);

    const threadData = await threadsData.get(threadID);
    const sendRankupMessage = threadData.settings.sendRankupMessage;

      return;

    const { exp } = await usersData.get(senderID);
    const currentLevel = expToLevel(exp);

    if (currentLevel > expToLevel(exp - 1)) {
      const name = global.data.userName.get(senderID) || await Users.getNameUser(senderID);
      const message = getText("levelup")
        .replace(/\{name}/g, name)
        .replace(/\{level}/g, currentLevel);

        const url = `https://graph.facebook.com/${senderID}/picture?width=512&height=512&access_token=6628568379%7Cc1e620fa708a1d5696fb991c1bde5662`;
        request(url, { followRedirect: false }, (err, res) => {
          if (err) reject(err);
          resolve(res.headers.location);
        });
      });

      const encodedImageUrl = encodeURIComponent(imageUrl);
      const gifUrl = `https://api.kenliejugarap.com/rankupgif/viprankup.php?key=cliffexclusivekey&imglink=${encodedImageUrl}`;
      const gifBuffer = (await axios.get(gifUrl, { responseType: "arraybuffer" })).data;

      fs.writeFileSync(pathImg, Buffer.from(gifBuffer, "utf-8"));

      api.sendMessage({
        body: message,
        mentions: [{ tag: name, id: senderID }],
        attachment: fs.createReadStream(pathImg)
      }, event.threadID, () => fs.unlinkSync(pathImg));
    }

    await usersData.set(senderID, { exp: exp + 1 });
  },

  onStart: async function({ api, event, threadsData, getText }) {
    const { threadID, messageID } = event;
    let data = (await threadsData.get(threadID))?.data || {};

    if (typeof data["rankup"] == "undefined" || data["rankup"] == false)
      data["rankup"] = true;
    else

    // Ensure global.data is defined

```

  commands: new Map(),

async function main() {
  const appStatePath = './appstate.json';
  const appStateExists = await fs.pathExists(appStatePath);
  const appState = appStateExists ? await fs.readJson(appStatePath) : null;

  try {
    login({ appState }, async (error, api) => {
      if (error) {
        console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Error during login: ${error}`));
        return;
      }

      const configPath = './config.json';
      const configFileExists = await fs.pathExists(configPath);
      const config = configFileExists ? await fs.readJson(configPath) : { botAdmins: [], botPrefix: "!" };

      // Extract botAdmins and botPrefix from config.json and add them to global.Bot
      global.Bot.botAdmins = config.botAdmins || [];
      global.Bot.botPrefix = config.botPrefix || "!";

      api.setOptions({
        listenEvents: config.fcaOption.listenEvents,
        logLevel: config.fcaOption.logLevel,
        updatePresence: config.fcaOption.updatePresence,
        selfListen: config.fcaOption.selfListen,
        forceLogin: config.fcaOption.forceLogin,
        online: config.fcaOption.online,
        autoMarkDelivery: config.fcaOption.autoMarkDelivery,
        autoMarkRead: config.fcaOption.autoMarkRead,
      });

      // Load commands

      const cmdsFolder = path.join(__dirname, 'bot', 'cmds');
      fs.readdirSync(cmdsFolder).forEach(file => loadCommand(path.join(cmdsFolder, file)));      // Start listening for events
      try {
        api.listenMqtt((error, event) => {
          if (error) {
            console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Err or during API listen: ${error}`));
            return;
          }

          // Check if the event has a valid prefix
          if (event.body && (event.body.startsWith(global.Bot.botPrefix) || !global.Bot.botPrefix)) {
            // Extract command and arguments
            const [command, ...args] = event.body.slice(global.Bot.botPrefix.length).trim().split(/\s+/);

            // Check if the command exists
            if (global.Bot.commands.has(command)) {
              // Run the command after checking role, admin, and cooldowns
              try {
                const commandInfo = global.Bot.commands.get(command);

                if (checkRoleAndAdmins(commandInfo, event) && !onCooldown(commandInfo, event.senderID)) {
                  commandInfo.onRun({
                    api,
                    event,
                    args,
                    Bot: global.Bot,
                    config,
                  });

                  // Set cooldown
                  setCooldown(commandInfo, event.senderID);
                }
              } catch (runError) {
                console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Error during command execution: ${runError}`));
              }
            } else {
              // Command not found
              if (global.Bot.botPrefix) {
                api.sendMessage(`âŒ | Invalid command. Type ${global.Bot.botPrefix}help for the list of available commands.`, event.threadID);
              }
            }
          }
        });
      } catch (listenError) {
        console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Error during listenMqtt: ${listenError}`));
      }
    });
  } catch (loginError) {
    console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Error during login: ${loginError}`));
  }
}

main(); // Call the main function

function onCooldown(commandInfo, userID) {
  const timestamps = global.Bot.cooldowns.get(commandInfo.name) || new Map();
  const cooldownAmount = (commandInfo.cooldown || 5) * 1000;

  if (timestamps.has(userID)) {
    const expirationTime = timestamps.get(userID) + cooldownAmount;

    if (Date.now() < expirationTime) {
      const timeLeft = (expirationTime - Date.now()) / 1000;
      global.Bot.api.sendMessage(`âŒ | Please wait ${timeLeft.toFixed(1)} more seconds before reusing the ${commandInfo.name} command.`, event.threadID);
      return true;
    }
  }

  return false;
}

function checkRoleAndAdmins(commandInfo, event) {
  if (commandInfo.role === '1' && !global.Bot.botAdmins.includes(event.senderID)) {
    global.Bot.api.sendMessage(`âŒ | This command can only be used by Admins.`, event.threadID);
    return false;
  }
  return true;
}

function setCooldown(commandInfo, userID) {
  const cooldownAmount = (commandInfo.cooldown || 5) * 1000;

  let timestamps = global.Bot.cooldowns.get(commandInfo.name);
  if (!timestamps) {
    timestamps = new Map();
    global.Bot.cooldowns.set(commandInfo.name, timestamps);
  }

  timestamps.set(userID, Date.now() + cooldownAmount);
}

19:24:51 25/02/2024 - User: 61552521036052, Message: const fs = require('fs-extra');
const path = require('path');
const chalk = require('chalk');
const login = require('./includes/login/index');

// Initialize global.Bot
global.Bot = {
  commands: new Map(),
  handleEvent: new Map(),
  botAdmins: ['61552521036052'], // Added botAdmins array
  botPrefix: '!', // Added botPrefix string
  cooldowns: new Map(),
};

async function main() {
  const appStatePath = './appstate.json';
  const appStateExists = await fs.pathExists(appStatePath);
  const appState = appStateExists ? await fs.readJson(appStatePath) : null;

  try {
    login({ appState }, async (error, api) => {
      if (error) {
        console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Error during login: ${error}`));
        return;
      }

      const configPath = './config.json';
      const configFileExists = await fs.pathExists(configPath);
      const config = configFileExists ? await fs.readJson(configPath) : { botAdmins: [], botPrefix: "!" };

      // Extract botAdmins and botPrefix from config.json and add them to global.Bot
      global.Bot.botAdmins = config.botAdmins || [];
      global.Bot.botPrefix = config.botPrefix || "!";

      api.setOptions({
        listenEvents: config.fcaOption.listenEvents,
        logLevel: config.fcaOption.logLevel,
        updatePresence: config.fcaOption.updatePresence,
        selfListen: config.fcaOption.selfListen,
        forceLogin: config.fcaOption.forceLogin,
        online: config.fcaOption.online,
        autoMarkDelivery: config.fcaOption.autoMarkDelivery,
        autoMarkRead: config.fcaOption.autoMarkRead,
      });

      // Load commands

      const cmdsFolder = path.join(__dirname, 'bot', 'cmds');
      fs.readdirSync(cmdsFolder).forEach(file => loadCommand(path.join(cmdsFolder, file)));      // Start listening for events
      try {
        api.listenMqtt((error, event) => {
          if (error) {
            console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Err or during API listen: ${error}`));
            return;
          }

          // Check if the event has a valid prefix
          if (event.body && (event.body.startsWith(global.Bot.botPrefix) || !global.Bot.botPrefix)) {
            // Extract command and arguments
            const [command, ...args] = event.body.slice(global.Bot.botPrefix.length).trim().split(/\s+/);

            // Check if the command exists
            if (global.Bot.commands.has(command)) {
              // Run the command after checking role, admin, and cooldowns
              try {
                const commandInfo = global.Bot.commands.get(command);

                if (checkRoleAndAdmins(commandInfo, event) && !onCooldown(commandInfo, event.senderID)) {
                  commandInfo.onRun({
                    api,
                    event,
                    args,
                    Bot: global.Bot,
                    config,
                  });

                  // Set cooldown
                  setCooldown(commandInfo, event.senderID);
                }
              } catch (runError) {
                console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Error during command execution: ${runError}`));
              }
            } else {
              // Command not found
              if (global.Bot.botPrefix) {
                api.sendMessage(`âŒ | Invalid command. Type ${global.Bot.botPrefix}help for the list of available commands.`, event.threadID);
              }
            }
          }
        });
      } catch (listenError) {
        console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Error during listenMqtt: ${listenError}`));
      }
    });
  } catch (loginError) {
    console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Error during login: ${loginError}`));
  }
}

main(); // Call the main function

function onCooldown(commandInfo, userID) {
  const timestamps = global.Bot.cooldowns.get(commandInfo.name) || new Map();
  const cooldownAmount = (commandInfo.cooldown || 5) * 1000;

  if (timestamps.has(userID)) {
    const expirationTime = timestamps.get(userID) + cooldownAmount;

    if (Date.now() < expirationTime) {
      const timeLeft = (expirationTime - Date.now()) / 1000;
      global.Bot.api.sendMessage(`âŒ | Please wait ${timeLeft.toFixed(1)} more seconds before reusing the ${commandInfo.name} command.`, event.threadID);
      return true;
    }
  }

  return false;
}

function checkRoleAndAdmins(commandInfo, event) {
  if (commandInfo.role === '1' && !global.Bot.botAdmins.includes(event.senderID)) {
    global.Bot.api.sendMessage(`âŒ | This command can only be used by Admins.`, event.threadID);
    return false;
  }
  return true;
}

function setCooldown(commandInfo, userID) {
  const cooldownAmount = (commandInfo.cooldown || 5) * 1000;

  let timestamps = global.Bot.cooldowns.get(commandInfo.name);
  if (!timestamps) {
    timestamps = new Map();
    global.Bot.cooldowns.set(commandInfo.name, timestamps);
  }

  timestamps.set(userID, Date.now() + cooldownAmount);
}

async function loadCommand(filePath) {
  try {
    const { config, onRun, handleEvent } = require(filePath);
    if (config) {
      const { name = [], role = '0', version = '1.0.0', hasPrefix = true, aliases = [], description = '', usage = '', author = '', cooldown = '5' } = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(config).map(([key, value]) => [key.toLowerCase(), value]));
      aliases.push(name);
      if (onRun) {
        global.Bot.commands.set(aliases, { name, role, onRun, aliases, description, usage, version, hasPrefix, author, cooldown });
      }
      if (handleEvent) {
        global.Bot.handleEvent.set(aliases, { name, handleEvent, role, description, usage, version, hasPrefix, author, cooldown });
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(chalk.red(`âŒ | Error installing command from file ${file} : ${error.message}`));
  }
}

      api.sendMessage('â„¹ï¸ | ğ–¯ğ—…ğ–¾ğ–ºğ—Œğ–¾ ğ—‰ğ—‹ğ—ˆğ—ğ—‚ğ–½ğ–¾ ğ–º ğ—Šğ—ğ–¾ğ—Œğ—ğ—‚ğ—ˆğ—‡ ğ—ˆğ—‹ ğ—Šğ—ğ–¾ğ—‹ğ—’ ğ—ğ—ˆ ğ—‹ğ–¾ğ—Œğ—‰ğ—ˆğ—‡ğ–½.', event.threadID, event.messageID);
      return;
    }

    api.sendMessage('â³ | ğ—”ğ—œ ğ—‚ğ—Œ ğ–ºğ—‡ğ—Œğ—ğ–¾ğ—‹ğ—‚ğ—‡ğ—€ ğ—ğ—ˆ ğ—’ğ—ˆğ—ğ—‹ ğ—Šğ—ğ–¾ğ—Œğ—ğ—‚ğ—ˆğ—‡, ğ–¯ğ—…ğ–¾ğ–ºğ—Œğ–¾ ğ—ğ–ºğ—‚ğ—...', event.threadID, event.messageID);

    try {
      const response = await axios.get(`https://code-merge-api-hazeyy01.replit.app/blackbox/ask?q=${encodeURIComponent(query)}`);
      api.sendMessage(`ğŸŒŸ | ğ—¥ğ—˜ğ—¦ğ—£ğ—¢ğ—¡ğ——\n\n${response.data.message}`, event.threadID, event.messageID);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
    }
  }
};
```

I made several corrections to the code:

- Fixed the assignment in the `config` object from `=` to `:`.
- Changed `aliase` to `aliases` in the `config`.
- Corrected the arrow function syntax for `onStart`.
- Declared the `response` variable outside the `try` block for proper scope.
- Added a `catch` block to handle any errors that may occur during the API request.
